  <raw>Nardelli named Chrysler CEO




Cerberus Capital Management picks an outsider to head the newly independent automaker.

Cerberus Capital Management LP late Sunday, Aug. 5, tapped former Home Depot Inc. chief Robert Nardelli to head Chrysler Group. The move came two days after the private equity firm closed its $7.4 billion purchase of an 80% stake in Chrysler from DaimlerChrysler AG.

United Auto Workers leaders approved Nardelli's selection, reports said. But Reuters quoted Canadian Auto Workers president Buzz Hargrove Monday saying he was "surprised and concerned" at the appointment and will seek assurances from Nardelli about Chrysler's Canadian operations.
Nardelli had been the high-flying and highly paid chairman, president and CEO of Home Depot until early January, when he was forced to step down after criticism of his rich pay package and the retailer's poor performance.
Before Home Depot, Nardelli had been a senior executive at General Electric Co. The appointment of a CEO with no background in the auto industry appeared to signal an effort to bring fresh blood into the company as it becomes independent. Cerberus has, however, named Wolfgang Bernhard, who had been a senior executive at DaimlerChrysler and Volkswagen AG, as Chrysler's chairman.
Chief operating officer Eric Ridenour will leave Chrysler after 23 years, the automaker said.

http://www.TheDeal.com</raw>
